If the puppet regime actually seizes postal rights in the Northeast, the authorities are prepared to withdraw all over four thousand postal workers to within the customs barrier and close postal services in the Northeast.

Partial Strike by Chinese Medicine Industry Yesterday 123

Feng Cunren Hall Workers Strike

Emergency Meeting of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union

Employer Representatives Petitioned Yesterday

The Dagong News reports that after a labor dispute arose in the local Chinese medicine industry, government agencies are seeking a proper solution. However, starting at midnight the night before last, workers at Feng Cunren Hall medicine shop suddenly announced a partial strike because their demands for bonuses were not met. The labor unrest has intensified and may escalate. Details are as follows:

Reasons for the Strike The workers at Feng Cunren Hall, citing low wages and difficult living conditions, submitted a request to manager Feng Jinpu the day before yesterday, asking for bonuses to be issued. Manager Feng considered the workers' demands unreasonable and refused to accept them. As a result, all the workers were indignant and believed that the shop was the first to violate labor-management conditions. Having now refused the workers' demands, over fifty workers collectively left the shop and declared a strike after midnight the night before last, and immediately organized a strike committee to direct everything. They also reported to the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union for assistance.

Letter to All Sectors The Feng Cunren Subgroup of the Second District Branch of the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union issued a letter to fellow workers and all sectors, declaring a strike. It stated: "To fellow workers and all sectors, the city's pharmaceutical industry has recently experienced labor disputes due to labor-management conditions. Our workers are united in protecting the conditions and fighting to the death for them. While these negotiations are underway, we hope that all fellow workers will work together with a unified stance. There should be no individual actions, but the rapid changes in the situation are unexpected. With the consent of all members of the Wood Subgroup this morning, we have implemented a departure from the shop to prompt our employer to reflect. Therefore, we announce the reasons, facts, and preconditions to all sectors and all fellow workers to clarify the truth. The employer of this shop has always been a strong member of the Pharmaceutical Merchants' Association and a champion of oppressing fellow workers in this industry. Feng Cunren, Cai Tongde, and Ye Tiande were the first to violate labor-management conditions. After the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union sent letters of warning based on the resolution of the delegates' meeting, the employer knew that it would be difficult to respond and asked the Merchants' Association to respond on its behalf, shifting responsibility to the Merchants' Association rather than the shop's own actions. It should be known that before the Merchants' Association notified all shops to reject external substitutes, the shop had already refused to send them. After receiving the warning from the Workers' Union, Cai Tongde and Ye Tiande had successively complied, but this shop did not. Moreover, other violations of conditions, such as relying on large bonuses (falsely claiming that there were few profits and not opening the accounts for inspection), are all violations of the conditions. After several negotiations, they have not awakened at all, but instead treat the workers in this shop as enemies, resorting to scolding at every turn. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? They even rely on the military force of imperialism to bully fellow Chinese of the same weak and small nation, thus provoking the public anger of all the workers in this shop. In order to cope with the environment, we had to leave the shop entirely to show our determination, while rectifying discipline and organizing a strike committee to deal with the employer of this shop individually. We hereby put forward two preconditions: (1) Substitutes shall be implemented as usual according to the contract. (2) Open the accounts and implement bonuses according to the contract. Other important issues, such as the overall violation of labor-management conditions, will be resolved by the Pharmaceutical Workers' Union as a whole. In addition to the problems of this shop, our colleagues will do our best for the three thousand fellow workers in this industry until the goal is achieved and we will never give up responsibility. We hope that all sectors and Wood industry workers will rise up and provide righteous assistance. We are extremely pleased."

Union Meeting The Pharmaceutical Workers' Union convened a special emergency meeting yesterday afternoon, attended by all directors and supervisors, as well as all members of the salary increase movement committee. Zhao Zhenhui chaired the meeting, and Zhou Dichun recorded the minutes. Discussions included: (1)...(2)...(3) Whether the Union should submit a request to party and government agencies. It was resolved to send Yuan Pinzhang, Chen Hezhi, Chen Yuantao, Zhao..., and Feng Xing... as representatives to go on the afternoon of July 3rd at 1:00 PM. (4) Whether to request assistance from the General Labor Union and various labor unions. It was resolved to send Yuan Pinzhang and the other four comrades to contact them. (5) Omitted. (6) Given the current dangerous situation, how to prepare financially if the strike is realized. It was resolved to levy a special donation on all members to prepare. (7) Secret. (8) Secret. (9) How should the Union respond to the Pharmaceutical Merchants' Association's proposal to form a joint committee to discuss and resolve this dispute? It was resolved that if the Association accepts the Union's preconditions, it will be supported; otherwise, it will not be involved. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Merchants' Association Petition The Pharmaceutical Merchants' Association, after a resolution by the Executive Committee yesterday, sent standing committee members Zhang Meian, Cen Zhiliang, Zhuang Meitang, and others to petition various agencies with a written statement. They first went to the Municipal Government, where staff member Huang Yunshu received them and promised to forward the representatives' petition points to the mayor for review and action in accordance with the law. They then went to the Social Affairs Bureau, where Section Chief Xu Yefu of the Third Section personally met them. After the representatives stated their petition, Section Chief Xu gave an important reply, stating that the Bureau attaches great importance to the current pharmaceutical labor unrest because of its profound relationship with society compared to any other labor unrest. He said that the root cause of the ups and downs of pharmaceutical labor unrest over the years lies in the imperfection of the labor-management contract. Therefore, the Bureau believes there are two ways to deal with pharmaceutical labor unrest: the symptomatic and the fundamental. Resolving the current dispute is the symptomatic approach. Reviewing the imperfections of the previous labor-management contract and having the government provide relief to make it conform to current laws and regulations, thereby facilitating compliance by both labor and management and permanently eliminating the source of all disputes, is the fundamental approach. The Bureau believes that for the sake of the permanent peace of society and the pharmaceutical industry, it should start from the fundamental aspects this time in dealing with pharmaceutical labor unrest. The Party Headquarters also holds this view, and so on. Later, they went to the Municipal Party Headquarters, where standing committee member Tao Baichuan received them. Tao's views were generally the same as those of Section Chief Xu, but he had a great deal of discussion with the representatives regarding the substitute worker system in the pharmaceutical industry. The representatives also stated their views as much as possible, and the representatives returned to the Association after a discussion until around 6:00 PM. From the above petition situation, it can be seen that the municipal party and government agencies have made concrete decisions on how to deal with the current pharmaceutical labor unrest. The labor unrest may not escalate for a while, which is good news for patients.

Merchants' Association Opinion The Pharmaceutical Merchants' Association believes that the most contentious issues in the four demands made by the labor side this time are substitute workers and placement. Therefore, the Association specifically expressed its views on the evolution of the substitute worker and placement systems in the pharmaceutical industry and the reasons why they should be abolished as follows: "The Shanghai pharmaceutical industry has never had so-called substitute worker and placement systems. They existed only from the 17th year of the Republic. In October of that year, the former Pharmaceutical Workers' Union proposed a labor-management agreement to the employer and made the acceptance of placing the unemployed a prerequisite for coercing the employer. At that time, the employer was under violent threats and, in order to take the overall situation into account, reluctantly accepted this harsh demand and placed 35 of the 116 unemployed workers in smaller pharmacies. The remaining 81 were used as substitutes in larger pharmacies. After this unprecedented bad example began, the Union again had more than 200 so-called unemployed workers and ordered the employer to place them all. Our employer believed that the Union's greed was insatiable and that the industry was in danger of collapsing, so it firmly refused to accept and vowed not to accept. Moreover, the employer had already completely resolved the problem of the over 100 unemployed workers last year, so how could there be so many unemployed workers again after only a few years? The source of these unemployed workers is ambiguous, which is already evident (the so-called unemployed workers this time are mostly unemployed in other cities and bribed the Shanghai Pharmaceutical Workers' Union to buy membership certificates and obtain illegal membership, or they work in small pharmacies in this city, are nominally unemployed, and hope to be placed in large pharmacies to obtain generous compensation. The identities are complex and cannot be investigated). How can the employer bear this undue obligation? Unexpectedly, the Union insisted on striking because its coercion was unsuccessful, lasting for 45 days. The employer almost went bankrupt, and society suffered all kinds of harm. Subsequently, the Central Executive Committee decided on a mediation method, the original order of which is as follows: 'The labor-management dispute in the city's pharmaceutical industry has been delayed for a long time and is very inappropriate. The Union (referring to the former Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Association) should be allowed to select from the 128 legally unemployed workers and introduce them to the employer for immediate employment of 50 people. As for the abolition of the substitute worker system, the 13 articles previously agreed upon by labor and management in the pharmaceutical industry have many inappropriate points and also conflict with the Trade Union Law. It should be resolved after the case is resolved, and the Trade Union should conduct investigations and studies and then submit them to the city's party and government agencies for proper revision to resolve and eliminate disputes. In addition to instructing the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters and Municipal Government to investigate and handle the matter, please inform them.') At that time, our employer, relying on the Central Government's instructions, in addition to complying with the order to employ 50 people, also issued each unqualified unemployed worker a one-time travel allowance of 20 yuan to return home, and completely dispersed and resolved the problem. It was said that from now on, the problem of unemployment in the pharmaceutical industry should not be revived, and the substitute worker system should also be abolished. Unexpectedly, the Union has raised this old case of placement and substitute workers again today. There are substitute workers after there is unemployment. The problem of unemployment in the pharmaceutical industry has been fundamentally resolved again and again, so there is no substitute worker in fact. How can the Union force the employer to use this historically abandoned term and create unnecessary disputes? According to the Union's excuse this time, the source of the unemployed workers is said to have come from the impact of the January 28th Shanghai War. In this case, the January 28th War was a national disaster. The pharmacies in the war zone were either bombed or burned down. How much more did they suffer from the national disaster in terms of losses and sacrifices than the workers who only suffered from unemployment? If the workers who became unemployed due to the national disaster are ordered by the employer to bear the obligation of placement and employment, then may I ask to whom should the employer appeal for compensation for the losses and sacrifices caused by the national disaster? Moreover, the unemployed workers affected by the January 28th National Disaster are not only in the pharmaceutical industry. Why does only the pharmaceutical industry Union have to order the employer to place them, while other industries are unheard of? Moreover, according to the investigations conducted by the Association, the number of those who were truly affected by the January 28th National Disaster and became unemployed is indeed very small. The Union is only taking advantage of the opportunity to absorb a large number of unemployed members whose identities cannot be investigated by improper means, and is only provoking the employer to cause trouble. What is its intention? It is self-evident. The social Mingda, fortunately, pay attention to it."

Silk Mill Labor Unrest 124

Social Affairs Bureau Summoned Both Parties Yesterday

Ordered to Attempt Reconciliation Out of Court within Two Days

Direct Labor-Management Negotiations Today

After the silk mill workers in the Hongkou district went on strike over wage issues, the unrest has spread to the Zhabei district. The Social Affairs Bureau summoned both parties yesterday to facilitate mediation and decided on three measures for labor and management to attempt reconciliation out of court. Details are as follows:

Total Number of Strikes After the Yichang Silk Mill in the Hongkou district went on strike, it spread throughout the district, including Tongwei, Yujing, Yuncheng, Xiangcheng, Xinlun, Yuanfu, Weiyu, Tongyi, Renji, and ten other mills. In the Zhabei district, Ruifeng, Yuji, Jiuji, Fengtai, Shenji, Fuchang, Heji, Yuanji, Xieji, Jiufeng, Dingji, Yuanhe, Zhenxing, Renchang, Tongchangtai, Chengtail, and fifteen other mills have joined the strike. The situation is expanding, and the sub-bureaus, sub-stations, and police stations in the Fourth and Fifth Districts have been ordered to protect the silk mills and step up security to prevent thugs from taking the opportunity to infiltrate. Currently, excluding the seven mills in the concession area and the three mills in the Nanshi district that have not joined the strike, a total of 25 mills have joined, with over 15,000 male and female workers. As for the silk mill workers in the concession area and the Nanshi district, it is reported that party and government agencies have taken measures to prevent strikes.

Details of the Interrogation The Social Affairs Bureau summoned representatives from both the silk mill industry and the labor side at 1:00 PM yesterday to facilitate mediation. Shen....Chen, Zhu Jingan, Zhang Peishen from the Silk Mill Industry Association, Zhu Xizhang, Yue Xiaorong from the Fourth District Silk Industry Union, Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Yang Gengdi, Yan Aizhu from the Sixth District Silk Industry Union, and Yang Shumei from the Third District Silk Industry Union attended the meeting, chaired by Wang Shui, director of the mediation section of the Social Affairs Bureau. First, the labor side stated that last year's wages were set at 5.8 cents. After the war subsided, Yichang in Hongkou was the first to start work, unilaterally reducing wages to 4.2 cents, paid every ten days, starting work at 4:45 PM and ending at 6:15 PM. Later, Tongwei, Yujing, and other factories started work one after another, all following the Yichang method, causing workers to feel pain and request the Union to negotiate. After consultation with the Industry Association, the Industry Association agreed to advise the factories on working hours and completely rejected wage increases. Now, in order to be considerate of the factory's side and maintain a spirit of cooperation, the labor side has proposed a flexible solution: wages of 5.6 cents and two days of bonus per month. The employer side stated that the price of silk this year is 50% lower than last year. Although the government has provided relief and all exports are tax-free, it is still not sustainable. Only 32 of the 113 silk mills in the city are currently open, which proves the industry's recession. In addition, financial institutions are unwilling to lend after the war, making it impossible to start work. Yichang's wages were negotiated by both parties themselves. This time, the strike was instigated by a third party, and the cause and responsibility for the strike should be investigated. After repeated persuasion by the chairman, it was still ineffective. Until 5:00 PM, the chairman decided: (1) The labor and management sides should attempt reconciliation out of court within two days. (2) If reconciliation fails, party and government agencies will formally mediate at 1:00 PM on the 5th. (3) The labor unions in each district will be fully responsible for the order of the strike. Thereupon, labor and management both expressed their acceptance and dispersed.

Negotiations Today The labor and management sides of the silk mill industry complied with the instructions of the Social Affairs Bureau and agreed at 5:00 PM when they dispersed yesterday to directly negotiate a solution at the Silk Mill Industry Association on Beishan Road at 3:00 PM today. It is reported that the Silk Mill Industry Association has decided to send Shen...Chen, Zhu Jingan, the Fourth District Silk Industry Union will send Yue Xiaorong, Zhu Xizhang, the Third District Silk Industry Union will send Yang Shumei, and the Sixth District Silk Industry Union will send Yang Gengdi, Wu Suzhen, and Yan Aizhu to attend.

Union Meeting The Dagong News reports that the Fourth District Silk Industry Union convened an emergency meeting at the Union headquarters at 2:00 PM yesterday, chaired by Chen Xiupu and recorded by He Yin. The report included: (1) The wishes and demands of the striking workers. (2) Senior officials of the factory stated that they did not participate in the strike after the factory closed down. (3) The Social Affairs Bureau convened an interrogation. Discussions included: (1) Workers declared a strike because of the factory's harsh treatment. It has been six days since the factory publicly closed down and threatened the workers. How should the situation proceed? Resolved: (A) Submit a request to the Social Affairs Bureau for mediation. (B) Send another letter advising the employer. (C) Notify the workers to wait for the authorities to resolve the issue. (2) Senior officials of each factory publicly represent all workers and express their opinions, acting......in order to......Resolved: (A) Report to party and government agencies to explain that the officials have other intentions. (B) Send a letter advising the officials that they must not take any action without the consent of the Union. (3) Factories belonging to the Sixth District Union also went on strike yesterday. Should personnel be sent to investigate? Resolved: Send...Sheng and He Yin to investigate. (4) Should the application for mediation be jointly handled by the Sixth District and Third District? Resolved: Solicit opinions from the Third and Sixth Districts. If there is no solution, apply independently. (5) After the labor unrest occurred, the outside world did not understand the truth. How should the public be made aware? Resolved: Publish a declaration.

New Executive and Supervisory Committee Members of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sworn in Yesterday 125

The second session of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's executive and supervisory committee members held a swearing-in ceremony yesterday at 10:00 AM. Those present included Executive Committee members Tu Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Lu Wenshao, Luo Qinghua, Zhu Wenqi, Bei Songsun, Chen Zeqing, Zheng Zeshang, Gao Shaoquan, Pan Xusheng, Yu Zuoting, Chen Yizhou, Ma Jiliang, and alternate Executive Committee members Xie Zhongle and Zhang Peizhen, totaling thirteen individuals. Also present were Supervisory Committee members Wen Lanting, Lao Jingxiu, Chen Songyuan, Jiang Zhigang, Du Yuesheng, Fang Jiaobo, and alternate Supervisory Committee members Zhang Yichen and Wang Boling, totaling six individuals. Representatives from higher-level organizations and various sectors included Mayor Wu of the Municipal Government, Tao Baichuan of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Wu Huanru of the Social Affairs Bureau, Xu Yiheng and Lin Jin of the Garrison Headquarters, Hu Hongji of the Health Bureau, Cai Zengji of the Finance Bureau, Lin Kanghou of the National Chamber of Commerce Federation, Zhang Liucheng of the Navigation Administration, and over a hundred representatives from the Silk and Satin Trade Association, the Sugar Trade Association, the Shoe Trade Association, the Western Pigment Trade Association, the Clothing Trade Association, the Tree and Firewood Trade Association, and the Fresh Meat Trade Association. The chairman was Wang Xiaolai, the recorder was Wu Jichun, and the master of ceremonies was Zhu Boyuan.

The Swearing-in Ceremony Procedure included (1) Ringing the bell to commence the meeting, (2) All executive and supervisory committee members taking their seats, (3) Publicly electing a temporary chairman, (4) Giving the highest salute to the Party flag, the national flag, and Sun Yat-sen's portrait, (5) The chairman respectfully reading Sun Yat-sen's will, (6) All executive and supervisory committee members swearing an oath of office, (7) Remarks from higher-level organizations, (9) Addresses from various sectors, (9) Addresses from trade association representatives, and (10) Adjournment upon completion of the ceremony.

Oath of All Committee Members: We solemnly swear that, with utmost sincerity, we accept the trust of all members of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, abide by the charter, diligently serve, refrain from seeking personal gain, and not neglect our duties. Should we violate this oath, we are willing to accept the most severe sanctions from all members. We solemnly swear.

Mayor Wu's Remarks: Shanghai is the economic center of the country, and is closely watched by various nations. Its position is important, and it has become the center of all undertakings. Therefore, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce holds a leading position among commercial groups nationwide. Let us observe the current situation in China. Politics, society, the economy, and the people's livelihood are all forming a highly dangerous situation for China's future. Our country is known as a country with vast land and abundant resources, but now it has come to the point where the people are poor, the treasury is exhausted, and the future is uncertain. The root cause lies in political instability. All kinds of undertakings in the country are not able to develop freely, causing the people's livelihoods to suffer from political and accidental oppression. Therefore, if we want to solve the safety of the people's lives, we must work hard to develop the national economy and promote the development of industry and commerce in various regions. However, within a country, relying solely on industrial production without cooperation with the commercial sector rarely leads to success. In the past, the failure of our country's enterprises was mostly due to the lack of concentrated capital. For example, someone starts a factory, and in addition to focusing on manufacturing, they also have to devote themselves to raising funds and promoting sales. Therefore, the difficulty of the domestic industrial sector is usually due to the lack of capital flow and the accumulation of products, which are the biggest reasons. If commercial organizations in various regions can properly guide their members to coordinate industry and commerce, then the above-mentioned difficulties can naturally be eliminated. If we want to seek social stability, the first thing to do is to nourish the national economy. The driving force of the national economy depends on the development of industry. The development of industry cannot be achieved without the commercial sector making every effort to support and promote it. Today is the day of the inauguration of the new officials of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. You all bear a major mission for the revitalization of industry and commerce in this city. Tiecheng offers the above opinions and hopes to work with you to promote cooperation. Then,

Remarks from the Party Headquarters Representative: Today is the day for the swearing-in of the new officials of the second session of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Your election as members of the Chamber of Commerce can be said to be due to the respect of the city's merchants. In the future, work hard to promote commerce and seek the development of industrial and commercial undertakings. Today, I sincerely wish you success in the future. We know that merchants have always had a saying, "In business, speak of business." However, this statement is not a bad thing. Industry and commerce are the engine of a country's economy. If industry and commerce can develop, the country's economy can be enriched and the country's position can be consolidated. However, in addition to this, in the current situation where domestic politics have not yet been put on track, the national economy is declining, and social conditions are unstable, merchants, in addition to their own responsibilities, should stand in the position of the people and seek national freedom and equality. Because industrial and commercial economy is only a part of the national economy, we should dedicate ourselves to society and at the same time seek a comprehensive solution to fulfill our responsibility to the country. The current system of election and appointment of the Chamber of Commerce holds a new-old replacement every considerable period of time. In this way, talents are rotated, and the cause remains the same. The future results will be satisfactory. I hope that you will work hard.

Remarks from the Social Affairs Bureau: Shanghai is the economic center of the country and an important area of the world economy. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce was formally organized two years ago in accordance with central government laws and regulations. The members, such as the various trade associations, are all sound organizations. In the recent past, they have helped the government maintain local order and have done a considerable amount of work. This is something we should praise. However, after the sudden changes in the local area, the vitality has been greatly damaged. How to adjust industry and commerce in the future and restore prosperity, and all kinds of facilities, need to be properly planned. Today, the old members of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce are retiring and the new members are taking over and being sworn in. The responsibilities they bear are even greater than in the past. I hope they will double their efforts.

Remarks from the Commander's Representative: Today, I am participating in the inauguration ceremony of the new members of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and feel a little bit of emotion. People say that China has a vast land and abundant resources, why can't it be rich and strong? I don't know the reason for this, because it is caused by poor politics and economic decline. A country, if it wants to be strong, must first have political power to the outside world. If political power is insufficient, then it must be supplemented by economic power. If both are prepared, then the country's position can be safely maintained. The reason why our country cannot join the international equal position and is bullied by the great powers is that it has not completed these two kinds of forces. In the past, we felt that the external forces were materially insufficient and that the guns were not as sharp as others. It was already like throwing eggs at stones, and it was inevitable that we would lose. In terms of economy, hundreds of millions of dollars are leaked every year, and we only feel that there is no way to make up for it. Since the 19th Route Army started to resist the violent Japanese with political power, it seems that we have given us considerable awareness. However, the use of political power is still based on economic power. Any changes in the world are based on economics as its background and its driving force. Only economy can transfer everything. If we want to save the country, we must have sufficient economic power. Just now, Mayor Wu said that we should work hard to develop industrial and commercial undertakings to enrich the country's economic strength. This is the urgent task of today. I hope that you will cooperate with the government and give the government the power of the people as a backing to resist foreign aggression.

Mr. Lin Kanghou's Speech: I served in the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce in the 16th year of the Republic of China, so I have a little understanding of the commercial situation in this city. But today, the situation of Shanghai's industry and commerce is declining and panic, which can be said to have reached the extreme. I remember that in the past, merchant groups did not talk about politics because their own organizations were not sound. Later, they felt that politics was not on the right track, and it was not easy to do anything well. So they began to ask about political issues. But for several years, the political variety has been on display, and the result is still fighting endlessly. Therefore, if we want to seek a way out for all undertakings, we should first stabilize domestic politics. Therefore, the anti-civil war movement that I recently advocated is our most important work. Although people have always appealed for peace whenever a civil war breaks out, individual actions have rarely been effective. Therefore, this time we are advocating the abolition of civil war, we must contact all parties, and we must first consolidate the organization of our own group, and not cause internal strife, and adopt various effective peaceful solutions to complete this task. So related to the hope that the Chamber of Commerce or branches, do not cause internal strife, then any future things are easy to cooperate, this is some of the ideas.

Mr. Wang Jie'an's Speech: After the end of the Shanghai War, although the military affairs have temporarily come to an end, the commercial war has continued. The economic strategy of the great powers has not diminished its ambition. We observe the imported goods on the market, and they are all dumped, almost to the point where our domestic products cannot gain a foothold. Chinese silk has always been the leader in the world, but now the domestic silk cocoon merchants are dying and have successively gone bankrupt. Looking back at Japan, it has spared no effort to promote it. This phenomenon is just like a soldier facing the enemy, not allowing retreat, while the Chinese merchants are in the final struggle on the commercial battlefield. Thinking about it, I can't help but feel vigilant. Today, the new members of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce are taking office. We merchants are still soldiers. From now on, we will wait for you to be in the position of officials, issue orders, stand on the same front, command us, and strive to attack, to embrace peace internally and resist to the end externally, in order to save a line of life for our country's industry and commerce. Finally, after the chairman made a reply of thanks, he announced the adjournment of the meeting.

to draft it, and it was passed and published by the executive committee, (D) The case of electing the convener of the standing committee members, it was resolved that the standing committee member Elected Officials: Five standing committee members of the executive committee: Qian Cangshuo, Yu Kongwo, Yan Esheng, Qu Shao'yi, Ma Chong, five directors of each department of the executive committee: "Organization Department" Zhao Junhao, "General Affairs Department" Jiang Jianhou, "Public Relations Department" Sun Daosheng, "Recreation Department" Hang Shijun, "Documents Department" Wu Zhongyi.

Russian Dies of Illness in the Detention Center of the Second Special District 127

French Concession Police Request to Hoist the Coffin for Examination

The Court Responds to Act According to the Agreement

A case of a Russian beggar, George Lati Lev, dying of dysentery in the detention center of the Second Special District Court on the 19th of this month. A portion of the foreigners in this city with ulterior motives took the opportunity to make an issue of it, so it was rumored for a while that the Russian had been beaten to death in prison. The French Concession Police also ordered an investigation, and in order to complete the investigation procedures, they sent someone to the Second Special District Court to request that the coffin be hoisted at the Tangwan Yizhongdi for examination. The court immediately stated that the court initially advocated opening the coffin for examination to clarify the truth. However, the court takes the law as its position, and all cases, no matter how small, must be carried out according to the law. The Russian was ill in prison, and there was already a coroner's report and a forensic examination report. The case had already come to an end. Later, the deceased's brother overturned the case and filed a complaint. However, the three Russians pointed out by the deceased's brother were questioned by the police one after another, and all denied witnessing George Lati Lev being beaten. Therefore, the evidence was insufficient, and the case could not be established. Under these circumstances, if the police are determined to examine the body, the court has no objection. However, it is necessary to determine who the plaintiff and defendant are in advance to clarify the responsibility. The police still need to send an official document. The French Concession Police sent an official document to the court the night before, requesting that the police be allowed to hoist the coffin for examination themselves in the name of investigation. The court stated that the right to examine the body belonged to the court's prosecution. The police hoisting and examining the body themselves violated Article 3 of the court's agreement. Therefore, this point is greatly related to China's legal rights and is difficult to accommodate. The court replied to the police yesterday morning based on this idea, so it is difficult to open the coffin for examination for a while. Xiao Jinfang, the secretary-general of the Second Special District Court, told our reporter yesterday that according to Article 3 of the court agreement, the examination matters should be handled by the prosecutor. However, in order to dispel the suspicion of foreigners, when the coffin is opened for examination in this case, the court intends to invite an international forensic doctor to conduct the examination together. The French Concession Police can also send another forensic doctor to participate at that time, in order to clarify the truth of this case. The news about this case is compiled as follows:

The Police Demand a Second Examination: Commissioner Faber of the General Investigation Department of the French Concession Police sent a letter to the Second Special District Court the day before yesterday, saying: "Sir, according to Si Meiweng Gelaji's claim, it is said that his brother, George Gelaji, died because he was beaten by an unnamed guard in the detention center. Based on this, a preliminary investigation has begun on the alleged perpetrator. In accordance with Articles 156 and 161 of the Criminal Procedure Law, it has been decided to appoint a committee to dissect the body, and Dr. Sandeli, a doctor from the French Concession Engineering Bureau, has been commissioned to handle this matter in accordance with Article 177. Detective Chief Xia Cai'er has also been commissioned to make a record. For this reason, I hereby request your court to inform the prosecutor to inform Tongren Fuyuantang that the body must be examined at the Taitelas Tuo Road Xujiahui Road autopsy site at 8 am on July 2nd. After George Gelaji's death, the coroner had already examined the body. If the prosecutor can ask the doctor to be present at the re-examination, it would be fortunate. The preliminary investigation will collect (1) the statements of the guards on duty in the section of George Gelaji's detention house when he was detained in the detention center, (2) the statements of the director of the detention center, (3) the statements of the doctor who treated the deceased, (4) the statements of the police officers who escorted George Gelaji, (5) other statements that can help to reveal the truth. The investigation will be conducted at the detention center at 10:35 am tomorrow (July 1st). To the Shanghai Second Special District Court, Faber."

The Court Rejects According to Regulations: After receiving the letter, the Second Special District Court, although it also hoped to clarify the facts as soon as possible for this bizarre case, and re-examine the deceased when necessary, the police's sudden request was not in line with the spirit of the agreement, and was fundamentally inconsistent with Article 4 of the agreement. Therefore, the original letter was submitted to the prosecutor's office, which rejected it with four points: (1) According to Article 4 of the agreement, whether or not to re-examine the body is the responsibility of the court's prosecutor's office. The police have no right to set a date without authorization, and fundamentally the time is too short and it is difficult to handle. (2) According to the police's settlement of the case, the deceased's original name was George Lati Lev. The name pointed out by the police now is George Grantki. The names are absolutely different. The police's settlement of the case stated that the deceased had no family, no wife, and no job, and made a living by begging. Now there is a sudden claim that the deceased's brother requested a re-examination. The court feels confused about the above two points. (3) In order to verify the truth of this case, the court may re-examine the body at the necessary time. At that time, the court will hire an international forensic doctor to be responsible for the examination. The police will be allowed to send personnel to participate.

The Police Begin the Investigation: Regarding the police's request to re-examine the body today, after the court rejected it according to reason, the police have not yet made any statement. However, the police's investigation procedures for this matter have already begun yesterday. At 10:30 am yesterday, the chief of the judicial section of the French Concession Police, accompanied by a recorder, went to the court to request to investigate the detention center. The court sent Secretary-General Xiao Jinfang to accompany them. The police investigated for an hour. All the detention center director Xu Rongwen, the medical officer Yu Minggao, and the detention center Ding were questioned one by one, and a detailed investigation was conducted in the detention center. In addition, the police authorities also interrogated Gao Faligao, a Russian who was released from the detention center the day before yesterday after serving his sentence.

Detention Center Director Xu Rongwen Spoke Strictly: When the police went to the detention center to investigate yesterday, the detention center director Xu Rongwen expressed his opinion on this matter frankly. However, after the police completed the investigation, Xu Rongwen asked the police, saying that when the police handed over the case to the court, the transfer form stated that he had no family and no job. After arriving at the court, the deceased also stated that he had no family and no job. Now, how can there suddenly be a self-proclaimed brother of the deceased? How can the police answer this matter? At that time, the police personnel could not answer.

Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau Investigates Household Registration in the War Zone 128

Population Reduced by More Than 800,000 After the War

Since the January 28th Incident, the household registration in this city has been extremely chaotic. Now, except for District D, where Japanese soldiers have not yet withdrawn, the rest have been taken over by the Municipal Party Bureau. The Police Bureau is deeply concerned that many undesirable elements may be mixed in. It has ordered the responsible district offices to re-register the household registration. The procedure is that the district offices or branch police stations first send household registration survey forms to each household, which are filled in by the households and sent to the district. The district then sends personnel to re-examine each household to verify the information and report it to the bureau. Now, the district offices are supervising their subordinates to actively carry out the work. Some of them have already completed the re-examination procedures, but it takes a lot of time to compile the entire statistics. It will take about the 20th of this month to complete the work. However, in the Zhabei District, because there are many Japanese residents, the bureau is responsible for public security and is also responsible for protecting the safety of Japanese residents in the city. Therefore, it should be investigated clearly. It has previously requested the Municipal Government to inform the Japanese Consul General to inform the Japanese residents in this city that they must comply with the regulations for registration. However, most of the Japanese residents still do not comply. Now, in addition to requesting the Municipal Government to make serious representations to the Japanese Consul again, we are still trying to proceed in order to complete the work as soon as possible. As for the number of households in this city, the survey conducted in December last year counted 397,859 households and 1,878,066 people. By April of this year, the number of households had dropped to 214,535 and the number of people had dropped to 1,056,113. The difference in the number of households before and after the war was 183,328, and the difference in the number of people was 821,953. This shows the huge losses suffered by the residents of this city in this war.

Yesterday's Hearing on the Arsenal Case 129

The Ministry of Military Affairs Approves Searching for Land to Build a New Factory

The Gun, Bullet, Machine Gun, and Machinery Factories to be Built First

The New Factory Design Committee to be Established Soon

The Shanghai Arsenal's issue of whether to continue or be abolished has, after Shanghai factory employee representatives Hu Sihong and others went to the capital to explain the pros and cons in detail to the military authorities, now learned that the factory received a telegram from the Ministry of Military Affairs yesterday, approving the relocation to Zhejiang and the search for land to build a new factory. As for the abolishment of the factory, it has already been dismissed. The New Factory Design Committee will be officially established soon. A reporter from the Datong News Agency met yesterday with Mr. Lin Weirong, director of the gun and bullet factory, who had returned to Shanghai from the capital. According to him, regarding the issue of resuming work at the Shanghai Arsenal, Vice Minister Chen had repeatedly telegraphed Chairman Chiang and Minister He to request instructions on the methods. Subsequently, they received replies from Chiang and He, agreeing to the resumption of work at the Shanghai factory and moving back to the old site. It was resolved that the entire machinery be preserved and a site be selected for building a factory, which could be approved. On the afternoon of June 29th, Minister Chen summoned and inquired about all construction and land purchase costs, setting a budget of 500,000 yuan, which is currently being raised and must be completed quickly. The location for the factory has been decided on the upper reaches of the Qiantang River, a place surrounded by mountains on three sides and facing the river on one side. It is planned to purchase approximately 300 acres of land to first build the gun, bullet, machine gun, and machinery factories, and establish a new factory design committee. The committee members have not yet been determined, and it is expected that the Ordnance Department will announce them soon. The authorities previously had considerable reasons for dispersing the machinery of the Shanghai factory to various factories, which cannot be criticized harshly. However, comparing the pros and cons, preserving the entire machinery and selecting a site to build a factory can take into account both national welfare and people's livelihood, which is more beneficial. Therefore, they were able to resolutely accept our suggestions. All parties are very concerned about the issue of the Shanghai factory's existence, but many reports contain discrepancies, which can easily lead to misunderstandings. For example, the details published in a certain newspaper on June 30th are not factual. I am the director of the gun and bullet factory, and I am more familiar with the process of relocating the machinery of this factory than others. A few days before the retreat of the 19th Route Army, I was ordered to rush to transport all the machinery to Hangzhou. Before the start of transportation, I sent Xu Yanru, a technician from our factory, to Hangzhou to find warehouses, borrowing two large warehouses at the Zhakou and Nanxingqiao Railway Stations successively before we could start moving the gun and bullet machinery and storing them in the Hangzhou warehouses to avoid damage from wind and rain. All machinery was oiled and painted. To prevent tipping, it was not packed in boxes (except for parts, which were not tied with straw ropes either). The claim that hundreds of yuan worth of machinery at the Shanghai factory was rusted is not true. As for the previous dismantling of the Fujian Arsenal, I was also the one who went to dismantle the machinery, transporting three sets of gun and bullet machinery and other ordinary machinery. After more than a year of sorting, they have all been installed and used, and there are no raw materials included, so what loss can be said to have occurred? In my opinion, if the construction of the new factory is rapid, it will only take more than a month to install the machinery. After the entire operation is up and running, the bullets and other products produced can reach the previous numbers, with no reduction. If the machinery were really scrap iron, why would we be so eager to request resumption of work? However, the machinery has been idle for a long time, and although it has been oiled and protected, I am afraid that it will rust over time, causing obstacles to future work, and a major overhaul will be necessary. Therefore, we are now planning to re-organize it once beforehand, so that it will be easier to start installing parts in the future.

Zhang Hongdu Sued by His Own Daughter

Zhang Hongdu Sued by His Own Daughter for Alimony 134

A Father Has an Obligation to Support His Children

The Father's and Daughter's Joys and Sorrows are Vastly Different

Zhang Hongdu, a native of Ningbo, made his fortune in business and has assets of hundreds of thousands. Recently, his own daughters, Zhang Xiuyun and Baoyun, hired lawyer Zou Shengzu to sue him in the First Special Court for alimony. The lawsuit states that the plaintiffs are the biological daughters of the petitioner. Since their mother, Guan, was forced to divorce the defendant in 1926, it has been five years. Because they are raised by their mother, they have not been close to their father. In the past five years, the plaintiffs have been able to feed themselves mostly because of a sum of alimony that their mother received from the defendant, totaling 2,000 yuan. Now, it has long been used up, and she has no ability to make more money, so they are constantly in danger of going without food. They believe that a father has an obligation to support his children. The defendant, with assets of hundreds of thousands, lives in a luxurious mansion, wears fine clothes, eats rich food, and enjoys himself fully. He alone endures the fact that his own daughters live in a thatched house, wear ragged clothes, and eat rough food. Speaking of this painful situation, they cannot help but shed tears. Therefore, they request that the defendant allocate the following funds: (1) Living expenses of 20 yuan per person per month on average, estimated until the age of 20. Xiuyun is currently 12 years old and has eight years until she is 20. Baoyun is currently 6 years old and has 14 years until she is 20. The total is 22 years, and 5,280 yuan should be allocated. (2) Educational expenses from elementary school to university total 6,140 yuan. It is estimated that the above-mentioned amount of litigation costs cannot be handled without hundreds of yuan. The plaintiffs' mother is a woman and has no savings. In recent years, she has become increasingly impoverished and now lives in the Chinese area in a very small residence. Even in the midst of fierce battles and the sound of artillery fire, she cannot afford to evacuate and can only huddle in fear. The bitterness of her situation cannot be described in words. Therefore, they seek a guarantor and request that litigation assistance be granted and that litigation costs be temporarily waived. The court approved the request. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Lou Ying opened the court for questioning. The defendant, Zhang Hongdu, did not appear and appointed lawyer Tan Xinzhen to defend him. After Judge Lou's interrogation, he ordered that the questioning be rescheduled.

Jealousy Murder Case in Moulin Street 135

Cohabitation Led to Ambiguity

Jealousy Ignited Murder

Yesterday afternoon, around 1:00 PM, a young man was stabbed to death in Moulin Street in the French Concession. The details are described below:

The Circumstances of the Murderer: Zhang Ruihe, also known as Ah Gan, a native of Huizhou, is 35 years old. He used to run a Huizhou tavern. He currently lives upstairs from a fruit store on Dongxin Street in the French Concession and usually enters and exits through the back door of Shoulu Lane. Sun Guisheng, a resident on the third floor of the same building, is married to a woman named Zhu, who is in her late thirties and of loose morals. She has been cohabiting with Sun for nine years and has two daughters, one four years old and the other two.

Helping the Woman Defend Her Husband: Because Zhu lived in the same building with Zhang Ruihe, they developed an ambiguous relationship over time. Sun discovered this. Three days ago, the couple had a quarrel. At that time, Zhang even helped Zhu against Sun, eventually resorting to violence. As a result, they were all taken to the Datong Clock police station. After the police chief reprimanded them, the matter was dropped. However, the seeds of murder were sown.

Waiting with a Knife: Yesterday morning, Sun went to Pudong. He returned to Puxi at noon and went to rest at the home of a fellow villager at No. 65 Moulin Street on Avenue Edward VII. Before even a quarter of an hour had passed, Zhang also arrived. Seeing Zhang, Sun's jealousy flared up. He quickly went downstairs and waited secretly at the entrance of the Zhonghua Lane to the south. Soon, Zhang also came downstairs. Sun suddenly pulled out a three-edged knife and stabbed Zhang in the left waist. Zhang fell to the ground in extreme pain. The murderer took the opportunity to escape.

Died from Severe Injuries: After the incident, a Chinese constable from No. 65 saw it and picked up the murder weapon. He took Zhang to the police station and transferred him to Renji Hospital. Because of his severe injuries, he died at 4:30 PM despite medical treatment. The hospital notified the police station, which sent detectives to transport the body to the autopsy room of the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home to await inspection by the court.

We believe that Taihu is a strategically important area of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and bandit suppression is a matter of utmost importance to the local area. Bandit suppression and pacification should be mutually supportive, and military affairs and administration are closely related. The area involves two provinces, and unified operation is essential. This relationship is extremely important, and the mechanisms are very subtle. A slight misstep can lead to many obstacles. After careful consideration, the positions of commander-in-chief and deputy commander-in-chief of the Taihu bandit suppression are not light responsibilities and are beyond the capabilities of Shaoliang and Yin. Furthermore, Shaoliang has been in the military for many years and has experienced many hardships. Yin has experienced many changes in the world and is increasingly aware of the dangers. Given the many difficulties of the times, we feel a deep sense of hidden concern. In accordance with the principle that everyone is responsible, we should strive to serve. Given the gentleman's heart of diligence, how dare we take on such a heavy burden? Rather than causing future mistakes and burdening your knowledge of people, we should honestly state our case and retreat in advance, knowing the difficulty. In our ignorance and clumsiness, we should avoid delaying important matters. We respectfully request that you consider our sincerity and allow us to withdraw our acceptance. We pray earnestly. Zhu Shaoliang and Chen Yin kowtow."

Newly Established Police Stations on Both Railway Lines 144

More than forty officers were appointed. The Police Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Railways directly established two police stations along the railway lines yesterday morning. Details are as follows:

Station Chief Assumes Duty: Yesterday morning at nine o'clock, the new Station Chief Ma Shaoping and Deputy Station Chief Li Dingrong, etc., went to the Two Railway Administration Bureau to discuss everything with Director Chen, etc. They then went to the Jielu Police Station to assume their duties. Yesterday, the interior of the station was still being arranged and had not yet been completed. It is expected to be ready today.

Personnel List: In addition to the Station Chief and Deputy Station Chief, the station's personnel includes one public prosecutor, four section chiefs. The chief of the judicial section is concurrently held by public prosecutor Li Jing, the chief of the administrative section is concurrently held by station officer Zhu Ciba, the chief of the administrative section is concurrently held by station officer Chen Tiewu, and the chief of the defense section is concurrently held by station officer Chen Junxia. There are four inspectors: Jiang Kaigeng, Wu Pingruo, Hu Yuanyi, and Yang Zhi'e. The personnel in the station are divided into eight ranks: station chief, public prosecutor, section chief, station officer, inspector, clerk, typist, and secretary, totaling more than forty people.

Police Affairs: The police stations along both railway lines are under the command of the Two Railway Administration Bureau and the Police Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Railways. They are specifically responsible for police affairs on the Shanghai-Hangzhou and Shanghai-Nanjing lines. In addition, the Songhu Railway, from Hangzhou to the surrounding area, is also within the station's jurisdiction. Currently, there are more than a thousand railway police officers, divided into ten regiments, distributed to various locations under their jurisdiction, commanded by the police sections of both railway lines. The police regiments are under the command of the police stations of both railway lines.

Ma's Brief Biography: The newly appointed Station Chief Ma Shaoping comes from the military, is thirty-two years old, and is from Taishan, Guangdong. He once served as deputy division commander of the 12th Division and regiment commander of the 36th Regiment. Later, he served as the chief of the security department of the Police Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Railways before being transferred to his current position.

Declaration of the Shanghai General Tenants' Association 147

The Shanghai General Tenants' Association declares that since the violent sun invaded Shanghai, launching attacks at midnight with airplanes, cannons, and flames filling the sky and smoke obscuring the sun, the people of the entire city fled empty-handed. Taking Zhabei as an example, the prosperous market city has been reduced to ruins, and the flourishing business areas have turned into rubble. Men and women have suffered such trampling. Such a disaster is rarely seen in history, and the extent of the loss can be known without further explanation. The association was founded in March of the 16th year of the Republic of China (1927). Residents of the city, believing that the revolutionary army had reached Shanghai and would publicize the reduction of the people's burden and implement the 25% rent reduction policy, organized this association one after another. However, in the initial stages, the regulations were not yet established. Fortunately, the municipal party headquarters convened a meeting and merged on the third floor to form the Shanghai Special Municipality General Tenants' Association, proceeding unanimously. In June of the same year, the government issued a notice prohibiting unwarranted rent increases, forced evictions, and the collection of digging rent tips, etc., all of which were on file. For several years, there have been very few disputes between tenants and landlords. Therefore, the association's affairs [blank space], but this time, with the Shanghai incident, the original branch associations have requested rescue and relief one after another. It concerns the tenants' demands to alleviate their personal suffering, and the association cannot remain silent. Therefore, a representative conference was convened yesterday to re-elect officers and take charge, sending letters to party and government agencies to send personnel to guide the discussion of methods for separately reducing and exempting rents this time, so as to implement them in reality. The rent in this city is the highest in the country. The level of rent should be based on the prosperity of the market. In the current state of economic depression, with the market factually closed to resist the enemy for nearly two months, all industries have stagnated, life is extremely difficult, and the burden is high. Rent has become a major social issue. Although residents in the Shanghai International Settlement and the French Concession are nominally safe, people without property have fled for their lives, abandoning their possessions and escaping alone, but without business or production, bearing high rents, it is impossible not to demand reduction or exemption. After the Sino-Japanese War and the Japanese earthquake, there were precedents for rent reduction and exemption. Now, the Jing-Hang-Beng-Zhen areas affected by the Shanghai war have already implemented rent reduction and exemption. How can the Shanghai war zone, so close at hand, have the entire city's tenants making such uniform moans and tragic appeals, and making requests that follow the rules and regulations, hoping to equally share the losses suffered in the war? After several months, no effect has been achieved, and no effective measures have been announced by the authorities. Although various groups have drafted measures, in addition to a small number of enlightened landlords who have automatically exempted rent, there are indeed many, but most landlords who only care about profit are controlling the courts, forcing evictions and demanding debts, and wielding power. Therefore, letters from tenants in various neighborhoods requesting assistance are pouring in like snowflakes. The courts, before receiving specific instructions, have no basis for how to reduce or exempt rents. The people of the entire city are suffering mental pain, calling out without response and appealing without [blank space]. The environment is forced to be like this, but there is no way to remedy it except to earnestly request the wise authorities to quickly stipulate effective measures for rent reduction and exemption. If it can be stipulated early, for the landlord, it will only reduce the current number of income, while for the tenant, it can relieve unlimited pain. What is most feared is that millions of people who are stretching their necks and looking up will continue to brew like this, wandering into divergent paths, which is contrary to social stability and market prosperity. We hope that the general landlords who do not understand will consider the feelings between the landlord and the tenant, clearly express their views, and no longer act coyly, procrastinate, and increase the mental pain of the tenants in the city. All tenants in the city will have a sense of gratitude for the favor. This is the declaration, and we hope for public discernment.

Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau Begins Issuing Certificates of Origin 149

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce previously approved a letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, approving a letter from the Polish treaty representative in China, stating that the proof of origin for goods exported from China to Poland has always been provided by Chinese merchants. Now, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of Poland intends to list the agencies in important Chinese commercial ports that issue certificates of origin, hoping for a reply after review and approval. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce also approved a letter from the French legation in China, stating that in order to implement the order issued on October 3, 1930, by the French government, all products such as live and dead poultry, grains and their accessories, sugar, raw sugar syrup, ordinary wood, gelatinous substances, essential oils and fats, essential oil acids, and fat acids must be accompanied by a certificate of origin before they can be imported into France. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce believes that the certificate of origin is used to identify the goods exported from the country and to prevent foreign merchants from counterfeiting. All countries have precedents. Therefore, it negotiated with the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to formulate eight rules for the issuance of certificates of origin, which were submitted to the State Council of the Executive Yuan for resolution and approval. Rule 2 stipulates that the Commodity Inspection Bureau or Inspection Sub-Bureau in various places under the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is the competent agency for issuing certificates. The certificate fee is two yuan in national currency per sheet. After these rules were distributed by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for implementation, in addition to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce informing the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, it also ordered the Commodity Inspection Bureau in various places to follow these rules. After receiving the order, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau started issuing the certificates yesterday (the 1st), and has sent letters to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Jianghai Customs, requesting them to check and inform all exporters to announce them to the public, and ordered the Ningbo branch of the bureau to follow these rules.

County Finance Bureau Announces Deadline for Paying Deed Tax 154

Approved by the Provincial Department of Finance, a one-month grace period is granted without penalty. The Shanghai County Finance Bureau announces that residents who sell and buy farmland and real estate should pay the deed tax within three months of the contract. Those who fail to pay within the time limit will be penalized according to regulations. This year, due to the war in Shanghai, residents were busy moving and avoiding the situation, and there were many white deeds that exceeded the time limit without being taxed. Now that the situation has stabilized, they should go to the bureau to pay. Considering the special circumstances this time, many households did not pay the deed tax because they were too hasty and had no time to take care of it, which is excusable. It has been submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance for special consideration, and all unpaid contracts in the county will be granted a grace period without penalty for one month, regardless of the date of the contract, to show sympathy. The order of the Provincial Department of Finance has been approved. In addition to sending personnel to conduct strict inspections, the bureau has announced to the county's households yesterday that they must bring the deeds to the bureau to pay the tax within one month from the date of the announcement, and they will be exempted from penalties.

Fan Zhaolan, a Shaoxing native residing at No. 179 Xiang'an Lane, Keneng Road, works at the Ministry of Railways. Recently, Fan Wu, a 22-year-old woman from Songjiang, hired lawyer Wu Chengyu to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Court, accusing him of seduction, abandonment, and injury. The lawsuit stated that the plaintiff came to Shanghai two years ago to make a living and worked as a cotton thread worker. The defendant began to seduce her. At that time, the plaintiff was only 19 years old and lacked knowledge, so she was seduced and rented a house. After living for about two months, the defendant rented a house at No. 52 Li'an Lane at the railway station. On August 21st of last year (lunar calendar), she gave birth to a son, and the defendant named him Fan Tao. He invited relatives and friends to the Hangzhou Hotel to celebrate the baby's one-month anniversary. On the first day of October, they moved to Keneng Road. However, when they moved in, the defendant had a mistress named Zhang living with him. The plaintiff was very unhappy and questioned him. At that time, the plaintiff's sister, Shen Wu, came to Shanghai and urged the defendant to hold a wedding. The defendant said that the child had already been born and there was no need to do so. The plaintiff had already made it so there was nothing she could do. From then on, their relationship broke down. On December 6th of last year, her son Fan Tao fell ill and died in a few days. She suspected Zhang. The plaintiff was deeply grieved for her son, so she often had disputes with Zhang. On June 17th, the defendant helped Zhang to beat the plaintiff. On May 2nd (lunar calendar), he forced the plaintiff to sign a letter of separation, saying that he would give her 200 yuan. The plaintiff refused, but on the 12th, the defendant beat the plaintiff and drove her out. She immediately reported to a lawyer and reported to the Huishi police station and sent it to Tongren Hospital for examination and injury, and instructed to file a lawsuit in court. In such a situation, the defendant seduced a woman under the age of 20, mistakenly believed that there was a marital relationship, and was happy to continue to commit adultery and have children. Fan Tao lived with Zhang and died within a few days, which is suspected of murder. After the defendant’s death, he said that he was beaten to death. He has already violated Article 257 of the Criminal Law of Seduction, Article 244 of Marriage Fraud, Article 310 of Abandonment, and Article 282 of the Criminal Law with Zhang on Murder Crime 293, injury, please punish according to law, in regard to the additional civil proceedings, should be compensated for 40 yuan per month, up to 60 years old, a living expense of 19,200 yuan, and because the plaintiff gave birth to a child and was abandoned, abused, and beaten, she suffered great mental pain and should be given a one-time consolation payment of 4,000 yuan, because the defendant works in the Ministry of Railways and does not have this ability." The court approved the lawsuit and ordered him to summon him. In the afternoon of the day before yesterday, the judge Feng Shide heard the case in the Second Criminal Court. The plaintiff and the lawyer Wu attended the court. Fan Wu stated the above situation. The defendant was interrogated, but he did not arrive. The attorney submitted a letter to the court, saying that the defendant was not in Shanghai and requested a postponement. Feng Yu approved the case and ordered another hearing to be scheduled.

To the Editor, Upon reviewing your newspaper dated the 27th of this month, I found a news item about the labor unrest in the pharmaceutical industry, which stated that "Jiang Hao, a special commissioner sent by the Central People's Movement Committee stationed in Shanghai, is investigating the truth in order to verify and handle the matter." The Central Committee has not sent any telegrams instructing me to investigate the labor unrest in the silk factory. The above-mentioned sections in the newspapers are inconsistent with the facts. When Puyi's concubine Wenxiu divorced him, Puyi agreed to provide 400 yuan per month for alimony. Now Puyi has broken the contract and has not paid a single cent. Puyi is clearly trying to shed his feathers. Wenxiu is very anxious and urgently telegraphed Puyi, asking him to remember their past affection and provide alimony. Puyi has not only broken the contract in this matter, but is also ungrateful and forgets his affection, which is too heartless.

However, during the Xinhai Revolution, the Chinese government also agreed to provide preferential expenses for the imperial family, amounting to 3 million yuan per year. Later, due to the government's financial difficulties, it gradually shed its feathers, which greatly affected Puyi's life. In the past, the Chinese government shed Puyi's feathers, and now Puyi is also shedding Wenxiu's feathers. Big shedding and small shedding, Puyi is really well-behaved and learns it right away.

According to Puyi's response, "The master wants to grant you death, and you still dare to ask for alimony!" Why didn't Puyi dare to say such a thing when he was in Tianjin? Now that he is covered by the name of foreigners, he says such sparkling nonsense, with the idea that "If the ruler wants his minister to die, the minister must die." But don't be too proud. In the past, the Chinese government shed your feathers. Who knows if the Japanese will not shed your feathers in the future?

Some surviving nobles and dignitaries are afraid that Wenxiu will drift around Tianjin and expose Puyi's scandal. They plan to jointly raise the current alimony. I don't think it is necessary. How can you poor and stingy surviving nobles and dignitaries afford this amount of money every month? In the end, you will inevitably have to stop shedding feathers. It is better to let Wenxiu drift around Tianjin, flaunt her beauty, and use Puyi's great name to attract lustful followers. Are you afraid that you won't get 400 yuan a month?

Puyi's flattery to the Japanese and Wenxiu's sacrifice for her love are originally mutually reinforcing things. What face is there to talk about?

[Science]

漂白粉製造法（下） 176

— 允釐

(3) Manufacturing procedures After the equipment and raw materials for manufacturing bleaching powder are prepared, manufacturing can begin. First, spread a layer of lime more than an inch thick on each layer of the box. Then insert the glass tube that conducts chlorine gas into the hole at the bottom of the box. It must be inserted very firmly so that no gas leaks! Then light the alcohol lamp and heat it under the flask, and chlorine gas will flow from the glass tube into the box, and be completely absorbed by the layers of lime in the box from bottom to top. After five or six hours, you must observe it through the glass window outside the box. If there is no color in the box, remove the glass bottle that produces chlorine gas, and stir the lime in each layer of the box with a stick. After stirring, pass in chlorine gas according to the previous method. After another five or six hours, observe through the window outside the box again. If you still don't see the color, stir the lime in the box again according to the previous method, and pass in chlorine gas again. If you see a yellow gas in the lower part of the box, this proves that the lime in the lower part of the box has absorbed enough chlorine gas. At this time, you must move the glass tube to the upper hole, close the lower hole tightly, and then pass in chlorine gas so that the lime in the upper part absorbs chlorine gas. Only when there is yellow gas in the entire box can the glass bottle for producing chlorine gas be removed and the chlorine gas stopped from entering the box. After this is done, the lime in the box becomes bleaching powder. This is a small-scale production method. As for large-scale production, many iron boxes are connected together. There is a horizontal axis in each iron box, and there are many teeth around the axis. When chlorine gas is passed in, the axis rotates slowly, which can stir the lime and make it evenly absorb chlorine gas.

(4) How to use bleaching powder Put the bleaching powder in a tank, first pour in dilute sulfuric acid, then add clean water to make a thin solution; then take colored cloth or paper and other items, immerse them in this solution, and then take them out and wash them lightly with clean water. Wash and then immerse it in the tank. After a few immersions and washes like this, the colored cloth will gradually become very white.

(5) How to preserve bleaching powder If bleaching powder is exposed to the air, it will combine with water vapor or carbon gas, which will gradually decompose and lose its bleaching effect. Therefore, it must be stored in a bottle or wooden box to avoid contact with the outside air. When using a wooden box, the inside of the box must be lined with thin lead skin; the seams on the outside must be soldered with tin, otherwise it will still be ineffective.

(6) Why can bleaching powder bleach? The reason why bleaching powder has a bleaching effect is because when bleaching powder is placed in a tank, it encounters sulfuric acid and releases chlorine gas to夺夺chlorine gas in the pigment, causing the original components to decompose and thus become white. Therefore, the effect of bleaching powder lies in pure chlorine gas.
