許先生的算術課 178

— 無畏

The class bell has rung, Mr. Xu, who teaches trigonometry, walks into the classroom with his briefcase. At this time, only one-third of the people are in the classroom, but experience tells him that there are always so few students in the ten minutes after the class bell rings, so he doesn't care and does his routine work - roll call - when the roll call is about to be finished, the students enter one after another, some with their mouths moving as they chew something, some with their trigonometry books, but at least a novel or newspaper is sandwiched in the book.

"Mr. Xu, No. X has arrived," they say automatically when they enter the classroom. Mr. Xu is probably old and has good self-cultivation, so he is not angry at all. He just says yes in his mouth, while his eyes and hands keep looking for the number to mark them present, but Mr. Xu's myopia is very serious, so it is easy for twenty minutes to pass like this.

Probably the common psychology is always to bully the good, they know that Mr. Xu is easy to bully, and his myopia is not shallow, those who are not good at moving read newspapers and novels, those who are good at moving talk about the Classic of Mountains and Seas, and sometimes they have to use their hands and feet to perform a full martial arts show. Mr. Xu always says with a smile: "Don't talk, you are not young anymore, you will graduate at the beginning of the year, listen carefully." These words are in vain, the classroom is still full of talking, unless the principal comes, it will be quiet for a moment.

At this time, Mr. Xu is facing the blackboard: doing a question, the active L, holding a slingshot: wants to use soybeans to hit S sitting in the first row, somehow, it hits the back of Mr. Xu's head, he quickly turns around to see who it is, but his eyesight is not good, so he is disappointed.

"Pigs! Really shameless, are you people? What::" Mr. Xu is angry, his feet

Page 22

Hitting the podium, his face turned red, L is very good, he quickly buried his head pretending to be reading.

At this time, the few who were talking: were confused by this, and stopped talking, so the air in the classroom suddenly became quiet. Mr. Xu scolded alone like this, feeling that he had no way to end, so his face immediately became peaceful again, he said:

"Don't mess around in the future, if you make me angry, I will scold people, if I get used to scolding in the future, everyone will be bored. We also talked, interrupted, and made the teacher happy when we were students, but not as good as you:: Okay, look carefully at the book, don't say in the future that Mr. Xu taught badly: making us not understand, in fact! It is you who don't listen, but the teaching is indeed what I taught, and you can't deny it, so everyone hurry up and listen carefully: don't make me old man embarrassed?" Everyone laughed loudly, and suddenly broke the quiet air.

Touching the Heart

大德里 179

— 嚴夢

I accidentally went back to Dade Lane on North Sichuan Road, which had once been a battlefield, with a friend who was moving things. The peach-colored girls on the street, dressed as flamboyant southern girls - my fellow fairies - are unfolding the smiles of youth in the car box or next to the road, just like scarlet spring flowers, rouge cheeks and lipstick, how moving is the temptation? The establishment of liquor stalls, the series of gold-selling caves, a coffee shop every five steps, and a dance hall every ten steps, oh, prosperous age, is it not in this that the reason why North Sichuan Road has become a mysterious road lies?

That bustling city area has now changed. When our tired feet stepped on that tired street, what we saw was nothing but a desolate rubble, the remains of the fire, the dilapidated walls, no longer the scene of the year. The blue-gray marines, the invincible yellow-clothed infantry, swaggered in the middle of the road, grinning and wielding messy steps. These murderous demons have been arbitrarily devastated in Shanghai, and now they are stepping into the Northeast. Their knives should be a new display - the blood of our nation!

We walked to Dade Lane with a sense of resentment. First, I went back to my home to visit, but besides the bullet marks and scars, it was as desolate as a gloomy ghost mansion. I mourned the canvas bed and writing desk and other things that resembled me for a long time, and nothing could evoke a deeper memorial - except for a lot of hard work that was scattered into manuscripts.

After hesitating for a while, I ran out from the back door, and as soon as I came out, I met a neighbor's wife who had been away for a long time. She asked me warmly about my life and the peace of the past - at the end, she earnestly asked, "Probably Shanghai will not fight again, right?"

"If I had known this today, why did I have to start a war in the first place?" She was concerned and felt pain, and I couldn't help but feel emotional when I heard it. She shook her head, sighed, and continued to ask me: "So what is Shanghai like? We women don't understand, do you know?" My heart was very sad at that time, and I didn't want to say anything more. So we parted ways. On the way back, I kept thinking: "What is Shanghai like?"

性的问题

Brawl 180

— Tang Zenggeng

On a gloomy rainy day, an incident occurred on M Road, instantly turning the usually quiet M Road into a hubbub of voices. Breaking the silence of the past, nearly every window had one or two or three heads sticking out, watching? The unfolding of this farce.

"Haha, look everyone, the jealousy jar has been broken!" In the quiet air, this cry rang out, followed by disorderly applause and women's scolding, creating a chaotic scene. This was the opening of the farce.

M Road was instantly dotted with many old, young, male, and female onlookers, especially in front of the door of a garage, where more people stood, surrounding it. Heads bobbed, and it was truly impossible to squeeze through. This was the origin of this farce. The area in front of the garage was the special reserved box, haha!

The main characters of the farce were two women with disheveled hair. They started by glaring at each other and finally resorted to a full-blown physical fight.

"You shameless harlot, who told you not to be a decent wife and come out selling yourself? Today you've met your match, I'll let you know how powerful I am, you shameless harlot!" The woman on the left cursed viciously, while rolling up her sleeves with both hands, preparing for a fierce fight.

"Don't even start, I don't know who's shameless. Why didn't you want a country bumpkin and had to come to Shanghai to steal my man, you slut, shameless!" The woman on the right said just as fiercely, also rolling up her sleeves.

"Pah, you cheap whore!"

"Pah, you rotten slut!"

They had already entered close combat. In a flash, the full-blown fight was about to begin. An uncontainable jealousy was burning in both of their hearts.

In a moment, the full-blown fight began. The large circle of people in front of the garage had now expanded, and in the center of the circle, the two main characters were tearing at each other, grappling into a ball, each hurling insults, drawing applause and laughter from the audience.

"Rip—!" The sound of clothes tearing.

"Snap—!" The sound of pants splitting.

"Haha!" Another burst of uproarious laughter. Hundreds of eyes were now directly focused on their breasts and vaginas, but on the muddy ground, they were still fighting desperately. Their disheveled clothes were covered in mud, and curses continued to pour from their mouths.

"Hey, officer, why aren't you doing anything?" A white-haired old man said to the policeman who was standing watching.

"Oh, sir, people say an honest official doesn't interfere in family matters. We don't take care of this kind of thing, haha!" The officer said, continuing to stare and laugh.

"Alas, people's hearts aren't like they used to be, morality is declining. We donate money so you can eat and watch fights? This is outrageous, alas, the dynasty is doomed!" The old man said sarcastically, slowly walking away from the officer.

"Hmph!" This was the officer's parting gesture.

At this time, the full-blown fight was still going on, but it wasn't as intense as it had been at the beginning.

After a short while, perhaps because the two generals were exhausted, they began to realize how exposed and ugly they had become. Therefore, they ceased hostilities amidst the cheering and laughter, still punctuated by their curses. A farcical play of a full-blown fight ended invisibly.

However, on M Road, the discussions were diverse, chaotic, and noisy, no longer resembling the tranquility of the past.

Criminal Judgments: Zhang Anqing and others' appeal in the Xu Jichang fraud case (Verdict): Appeal dismissed. ▲ Chen Xueshu's robbery case (Verdict): Chen Xueshu, as a co-conspirator in two counts of robbery by a group of three or more people, is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for each count, resulting in a combined sentence of eight years of imprisonment, deprivation of civil rights for ten years, and the deduction of one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention. The combined fine is twenty-four yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory enforcement, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for each yuan, and one yuan of the fine will be deducted for each day of detention. ▲ Kong Dengshan's case of disrupting family and public morals (Verdict): Kong Dengshan is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the offense of abducting a woman under the age of twenty with the intention of sexual intercourse and separating her from her parental authority, with one day of imprisonment deducted for every two days of detention.
